\hypertarget{data-import-and-preparation}{%
\section{Data Import and
Preparation}\label{data-import-and-preparation}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load all data files}
\NormalTok{demographic\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/demographic\_data.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{non\_nav }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/non\_nav\_data.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{ya\_nav }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/ya\_averaged\_results.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{oa\_nav }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/oa\_averaged\_results.csv"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Combine YA and OA navigation data}
\NormalTok{nav\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  ya\_nav }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group =} \StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{  oa\_nav }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group =} \StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Average navigation metrics across all blocks for each participant}
\NormalTok{nav\_averaged }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ nav\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(Participant, Group) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{Mean\_Speed =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(Speed, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{Mean\_Distance =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(Distance, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{Mean\_Navigation\_Time =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(Navigation\_Time, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{.groups =} \StringTok{"drop"}
\NormalTok{  )}

\CommentTok{\# Merge all datasets}
\NormalTok{merged\_temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ demographic\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{full\_join}\NormalTok{(non\_nav, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"Participant"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{suffix =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_demo"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"\_non\_nav"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group =} \FunctionTok{coalesce}\NormalTok{(Group\_non\_nav, }
                          \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(Group\_demo }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Group\_demo, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Group\_non\_nav)}

\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(nav\_averaged, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Participant"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Group"}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{\# Calculate change scores}
\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{SSS\_Diff =}\NormalTok{ SSS\_Post }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ SSS\_Pre,}
    \AttributeTok{SSQ\_Diff =}\NormalTok{ SSQ\_Post }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ SSQ\_Pre}
\NormalTok{  )}

\CommentTok{\# FILTER TO ONLY OA PARTICIPANTS}
\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(Group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# CREATE OA SUBGROUPS BASED ON NARA SCORE}
\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{OA\_Subgroup =} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(NARA }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{3.5}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA\_High"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA\_Low"}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{\# Display sample of merged data}
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Total OA participants:"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(merged\_data), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Create contingency table (original 3 categories)}
\NormalTok{handedness\_table\_original }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(merged\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Handedness, merged\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{OA\_Subgroup)}

\begin{Highlighting}[]

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Result: SIGNIFICANT difference in VR experience between OA subgroups (p \textless{} 0.05)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vr) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vr)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Direction: OA\_High has MORE prior VR experience (Median High ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vr), }
        \StringTok{", Low ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vr), }\StringTok{")}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vr) }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vr)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Direction: OA\_Low has MORE prior VR experience (Median High ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vr), }
        \StringTok{", Low ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vr), }\StringTok{")}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Direction: Medians are equal, but distributions differ}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Result: NO significant difference in VR experience between OA subgroups (p \textgreater{}= 0.05)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Median OA\_High ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vr), }\StringTok{", Median OA\_Low ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vr), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## Result: NO significant difference in VR experience between OA subgroups (p >= 0.05)
## Median OA_High = 0 , Median OA_Low = 0
\end{verbatim}

\CommentTok{\# Decide which test to use}
\NormalTok{use\_welch }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ levene\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Pr(\textgreater{}F)}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}
\NormalTok{use\_nonparametric }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ shapiro\_high}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05} \SpecialCharTok{|}\NormalTok{ shapiro\_low}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_nonparametric) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"⚠️ Data violates normality assumption. Using Mann{-}Whitney U test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  mw\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{wilcox.test}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg, oa\_low\_vg, }\AttributeTok{exact =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Mann{-}Whitney U Test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"W statistic ="}\NormalTok{, mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size}
\NormalTok{  n1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg)}
\NormalTok{  n2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vg)}
\NormalTok{  r\_rank\_biserial }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\DecValTok{2}\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ (n1 }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ n2)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Rank{-}biserial correlation ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(r\_rank\_biserial, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Report IQR for each subgroup}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{IQR by OA subgroup:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"OA\_High: ["}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg, }\FloatTok{0.25}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg, }\FloatTok{0.75}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"OA\_Low: ["}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vg, }\FloatTok{0.25}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vg, }\FloatTok{0.75}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_welch) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Variances are unequal. Using Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  t\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{t.test}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg, oa\_low\_vg, }\AttributeTok{var.equal =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"t ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size (Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d)}
\NormalTok{  pooled\_sd }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vg)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cohens\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_vg) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_vg)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ pooled\_sd}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(cohens\_d, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Assumptions met. Using standard independent samples t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Independent Samples t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"t ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_nonparametric) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"⚠️ Data violates normality assumption. Using Mann{-}Whitney U test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  mw\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{wilcox.test}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ex, oa\_low\_ex, }\AttributeTok{exact =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Mann{-}Whitney U Test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"W statistic ="}\NormalTok{, mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size}
\NormalTok{  n1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ex)}
\NormalTok{  n2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ex)}
\NormalTok{  r\_rank\_biserial }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\DecValTok{2}\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ (n1 }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ n2)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Rank{-}biserial correlation ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(r\_rank\_biserial, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_welch) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Variances are unequal. Using Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"OA\_Low: ["}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_psqi, }\FloatTok{0.25}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_psqi, }\FloatTok{0.75}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_welch) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Variances are unequal. Using Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  t\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{t.test}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_psqi, oa\_low\_psqi, }\AttributeTok{var.equal =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"t ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size (Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d)}
\NormalTok{  pooled\_sd }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_psqi)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_psqi)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cohens\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_psqi) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_psqi)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ pooled\_sd}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(cohens\_d, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Assumptions met. Using standard independent samples t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  t\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{t.test}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_psqi, oa\_low\_psqi, }\AttributeTok{var.equal =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Independent Samples t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"t ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}

  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_psqi) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_psqi)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Direction: OA\_High has WORSE sleep quality than OA\_Low}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}

\NormalTok{\}}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Independent Samples t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size (Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d)}
\NormalTok{  pooled\_sd }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_trails)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_trails)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cohens\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_trails) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_trails)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ pooled\_sd}

\NormalTok{  \}}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Result: NO significant difference in Trails B performance between OA subgroups (p \textgreater{}= 0.05)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"⚠️ Data violates normality assumption. Using Mann{-}Whitney U test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size}

\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_welch) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Variances are unequal. Using Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"t ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size (Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d)}

  \CommentTok{\# Effect size}
\NormalTok{  n1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_post)}
\NormalTok{  n2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ssq\_post)}
\NormalTok{  r\_rank\_biserial }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\DecValTok{2}\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ (n1 }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ n2)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Rank{-}biserial correlation ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(r\_rank\_biserial, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Report IQR for each subgroup}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{IQR by OA subgroup:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"OA\_High: ["}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_post, }\FloatTok{0.25}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_post, }\FloatTok{0.75}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ mw\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_welch) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Variances are unequal. Using Welch\textquotesingle{}s t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Assumptions met. Using standard independent samples t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size (Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d)}
\NormalTok{  pooled\_sd }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_diff)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ssq\_diff)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cohens\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_diff) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ssq\_diff)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ pooled\_sd}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(cohens\_d, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Assumptions met. Using standard independent samples t{-}test.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  t\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{t.test}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_diff, oa\_low\_ssq\_diff, }\AttributeTok{var.equal =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Independent Samples t{-}test Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"t ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"95\% CI for difference: ["}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{, t\_test}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{conf.int[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Effect size (Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d)}
\NormalTok{  pooled\_sd }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_diff)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ssq\_diff)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cohens\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_diff) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ssq\_diff)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ pooled\_sd}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Cohen\textquotesingle{}s d ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(cohens\_d, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{\}}

## df = 28

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Result: SIGNIFICANT difference in SSQ change between OA subgroups (p \textless{} 0.05)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_high\_ssq\_diff) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(oa\_low\_ssq\_diff)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Direction: OA\_High had GREATER increase in symptoms than OA\_Low}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Direction: OA\_Low had GREATER increase in symptoms than OA\_High}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
